\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Contains {\itshape low-\/level} functions and variables of the \textbackslash{}\+C\+Img Library. 

Most of the functions and variables within this namespace are used by the \textbackslash{}\+C\+Img library for low-\/level operations. You may use them to access specific const values or environment variables internally used by \textbackslash{}\+C\+Img. \begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Never write {\ttfamily using namespace cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg;} in your source code. Lot of functions in the {\ttfamily cimg\+:\+: namespace} have the same names as standard C functions that may be defined in the global namespace {\ttfamily \+::}. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Get/set path to the {\ttfamily curl} binary. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em user\+\_\+path} & Specified path, or {\ttfamily 0} to get the path currently used. \\
\hline
{\em reinit\+\_\+path} & Force path to be recalculated (may take some time). \\
\hline

Display a simple dialog box, and wait for the user\textquotesingle{}s response \textbackslash{}specialization. 

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a11aed0e6b30d75bf50946ee78d1aed94}\label{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a11aed0e6b30d75bf50946ee78d1aed94}}

\index{dialog@{dialog}!cimg\_library\_suffixed::cimg@{cimg\_library\_suffixed::cimg}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{dialog()}{dialog()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename t $>$ \\
int cimg\+\_\+library\+\_\+suffixed\+::cimg\+::dialog (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{title,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{msg,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{button1\+\_\+label,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{button2\+\_\+label,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{button3\+\_\+label,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{button4\+\_\+label,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{button5\+\_\+label,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{button6\+\_\+label,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library__suffixed_1_1CImg}{C\+Img}}$<$ t $>$ \&}]{logo,  }\item[{const bool}]{is\+\_\+centered = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Display a simple dialog box, and wait for the user\textquotesingle{}s response. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em title} & Title of the dialog window. \\
\hline
{\em msg} & Main message displayed inside the dialog window. \\
\hline
{\em button1\+\_\+label} & Label of the 1st button. \\
\hline
{\em button2\+\_\+label} & Label of the 2nd button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em button3\+\_\+label} & Label of the 3rd button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em button4\+\_\+label} & Label of the 4th button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em button5\+\_\+label} & Label of the 5th button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em button6\+\_\+label} & Label of the 6th button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em logo} & Image logo displayed at the left of the main message. \\
\hline
{\em is\+\_\+centered} & Tells if the dialog window must be centered on the screen. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Index of clicked button (from {\ttfamily 0} to {\ttfamily 5}), or {\ttfamily -\/1} if the dialog window has been closed by the user. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Up to 6 buttons can be defined in the dialog window.
\item The function returns when a user clicked one of the button or closed the dialog window.
\item If a button text is set to 0, the corresponding button (and the following) will not appear in the dialog box. At least one button must be specified. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{exception\_mode()}{exception\_mode()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily unsigned int\& cimg\+\_\+library\+\_\+suffixed\+::cimg\+::exception\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const unsigned int}]{mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Set current \textbackslash{}\+C\+Img exception mode. 

The way error messages are handled by \textbackslash{}\+C\+Img can be changed dynamically, using this function. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode} & Desired exception mode. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 0}\+: Hide library messages (quiet mode).
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: Print library messages on the console.
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: Display library messages on a dialog window.
\item {\ttfamily 3}\+: Do as {\ttfamily 1} + add extra debug warnings (slow down the code!).
\item {\ttfamily 4}\+: Do as {\ttfamily 2} + add extra debug warnings (slow down the code!). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a9414cac8b0ab20669320c37878fe54cc}\label{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a9414cac8b0ab20669320c37878fe54cc}}

Load file from network as a local temporary file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em url} & U\+RL of the filename, as a C-\/string. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em filename\+\_\+local} & C-\/string containing the path to a local copy of {\ttfamily filename}. \\
\hline
 & {\em timeout} & Maximum time (in seconds) authorized for downloading the file from the U\+RL. \\
\hline

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Value of {\ttfamily filename\+\_\+local}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Use the {\ttfamily libcurl} library, or the external binaries {\ttfamily wget} or {\ttfamily curl} to perform the download. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{minmod()}{minmod()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{UImg_8h_a0cff77f29b66e03bfc7e58ba80904457}{T}} cimg\+\_\+library\+\_\+suffixed\+::cimg\+::minmod (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{UImg_8h_a0cff77f29b66e03bfc7e58ba80904457}{T}} \&}]{a,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{UImg_8h_a0cff77f29b66e03bfc7e58ba80904457}{T}} \&}]{b }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Return the min-\/mod of two values. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
{\itshape minmod({\ttfamily a},{\ttfamily b})} is defined to be\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape minmod({\ttfamily a},{\ttfamily b}) = min({\ttfamily a},{\ttfamily b})}, if {\ttfamily a} and {\ttfamily b} have the same sign.
\item {\itshape minmod({\ttfamily a},{\ttfamily b}) = 0}, if {\ttfamily a} and {\ttfamily b} have different signs. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This modulo function accepts negative and floating-\/points modulo numbers, as well as variables of any type. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{openmp\_mode()}{openmp\_mode()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily unsigned int cimg\+\_\+library\+\_\+suffixed\+::cimg\+::openmp\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const unsigned int}]{mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Set current \textbackslash{}\+C\+Img openmp mode. 

The way openmp-\/based methods are handled by \textbackslash{}\+C\+Img can be changed dynamically, using this function. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode} & Desired openmp mode. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 0}\+: Never parallelize.
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: Always parallelize.
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: Adaptive parallelization mode (default behavior). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{wait@{wait}!cimg\_library\_suffixed::cimg@{cimg\_library\_suffixed::cimg}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wait()}{wait()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{CImg_8h_ae78061fec7a4c85b36265b3fac6ee928}{cimg\+\_\+long}} cimg\+\_\+library\+\_\+suffixed\+::cimg\+::wait (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const unsigned int}]{milliseconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Wait for a given number of milliseconds since the last call to \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a3e327ead14199e8de6bd67e096251a51}{wait()}}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em milliseconds} & Number of milliseconds to wait for. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Number of milliseconds elapsed since the last call to \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a3e327ead14199e8de6bd67e096251a51}{wait()}}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Same as \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_aa2bf8fb0d97c122cbc52e1f2e167e8a6}{sleep()}} with a waiting time computed with regard to the last call of \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a3e327ead14199e8de6bd67e096251a51}{wait()}}. It may be used to temporize your program properly, without wasting C\+PU time. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a3e327ead14199e8de6bd67e096251a51}\label{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a3e327ead14199e8de6bd67e096251a51}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_acfd3624d72ed7f79c82ec45646c685e7}\label{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_acfd3624d72ed7f79c82ec45646c685e7}} 
\index{cimg\_library\_suffixed::cimg@{cimg\_library\_suffixed::cimg}!warn@{warn}}
\index{warn@{warn}!cimg\_library\_suffixed::cimg@{cimg\_library\_suffixed::cimg}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{warn()}{warn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void cimg\+\_\+library\+\_\+suffixed\+::cimg\+::warn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{format,  }\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Display a warning message on the default output stream. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em format} & C-\/string containing the format of the message, as with {\ttfamily std\+::printf()}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If configuration macro {\ttfamily cimg\+\_\+strict\+\_\+warnings} is set, this function throws a {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library__suffixed_1_1CImgWarningException}{C\+Img\+Warning\+Exception}}} instead. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
As the first argument is a format string, it is highly recommended to write 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_acfd3624d72ed7f79c82ec45646c685e7}{cimg::warn}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"\%s"},warning\_message);}
\end{DoxyCode}
 instead of 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_acfd3624d72ed7f79c82ec45646c685e7}{cimg::warn}}(warning\_message);}
\end{DoxyCode}
 if {\ttfamily warning\+\_\+message} can be arbitrary, to prevent nasty memory access. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a36ccf2e6a6542f4e93eac819cf5d91ba}\label{namespacecimg__library__suffixed_1_1cimg_a36ccf2e6a6542f4e93eac819cf5d91ba}}
